std\+::string \mbox{\hyperlink{class_c_l_i_1_1_option_ab84751fbf9037efaed5b64fed17fe57f}{get\+\_\+name}} (bool positional=false, bool all\+\_\+options=false) const
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Gets a comma separated list of names. Will include / prefer the positional name if positional is true. If all\+\_\+options is false, pick just the most descriptive name to show. Use {\ttfamily get\+\_\+name(true)} to get the positional name (replaces {\ttfamily get\+\_\+pname}) \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}
